          WHEN 2 THEN 'AssistantManager'
          WHEN 3 THEN 'AccountManager'
          WHEN 4 THEN 'TeamLeader'
          WHEN 5 THEN 'Employee'
          WHEN 6 THEN 'Client'
          ELSE CAST("u"."role" AS TEXT)
      END, "u"."team_leader_id", "u0"."name", "u0"."user_id", "s"."DeptId", "s"."DeptName", "s"."user_dept_id", "u2"."user_id", "c"."client_id"
      FROM "USER" AS "u"
      LEFT JOIN "USER" AS "u0" ON "u"."team_leader_id" = "u0"."user_id"

          SELECT "d"."dept_id" AS "DeptId", "d"."dept_name" AS "DeptName", "u1"."user_dept_id", "u1"."user_id"
